ShouldSample(p tracesdk.SamplingParameters) tracesdk.SamplingResult {\n   376→\trl.Lock()\n   377→\tdefer rl.Unlock()\n   378→\tpsc := trace.SpanContextFromContext(p.ParentContext)\n   379→\tif rl.balance >= 1 {\n   380→\t\trl.balance -= 1\n   381→\t\treturn tracesdk.SamplingResult{Decision: tracesdk.RecordAndSample, Tracestate: psc.TraceState()}\n   382→\t}\n   383→\tcurrentTime := rl.balance >= 1 {\n   388→\t\trl.balance -= 1\n   389→\t\treturn tracesdk.SamplingResult{Decision: tracesdk.RecordAndSample, Tracestate: psc.TraceState()}\n   390→\t}\n   391→\treturn 31→// Start creates spans using both OpenTelemetry, and the k8s.io/utils/trace package.\n    32→// It only creates an OpenTelemetry span if the incoming context already includes a span.\n    33→func Start(ctx context.Context, name string, attributes ...attribute.KeyValue) (context.Context, *Span) {\n    34→\t// If the incoming context already includes an OpenTelemetry span, create a child span with the provided name and attributes.\n    35→\t// If the caller is not using OpenTelemetry, or has tracing disabled (e.g. with a component-specific feature flag), this is a noop.\n    36→\tctx, otelSpan := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx).TracerProvider().Tracer(instrumentationScope).Start(ctx, name, trace.WithAttributes(attributes...))\n    37→\t// If there is already a utiltrace span in the context, use that as our parent span.\n    38→\tutilSpan := utiltrace.FromContext(ctx).Nest(name, attributesToFields(attributes)...)\n    39→\t// Set the trace as active in the context so that subsequent Start calls create nested spans.\n    40→\treturn utiltrace.ContextWithTrace(ctx, utilSpan), &Span{\n    41→\t\totelSpan: otelSpan,\n    42→\t\tutilSpan: utilSpan,\n    43→\t}\n    44→}\n OpenTelemetry (otel) and Jaeger propagators. In Grafana, the central tracing infrastructure is in `pkg/infra/tracing/tracing.go`, which manages TracingService initialization with support for both Jaeger and W3C TraceContext propagators. The `Inject()` method (line 345-347) uses `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Inject(ctx, propagation.HeaderCarrier(header))` to inject trace context into HTTP headers. Context extraction from incoming requests is handled in multiple layers: `pkg/middleware/request_tracing.go` (line 103) uses `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Extract()` for server-side request tracing, `pkg/apiserver/endpoints/filters/jaeger_tracing.go` (line 14) specifically extracts Jaeger trace context, and `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/tracing.go` (line 19) extracts context from gRPC metadata. The `Run()` method (line 62) registers the global TextMapPropagator as `propagation.TraceContext{}`.
